If you have the PRO upgrade it’s possible to save it to a GPS exchange file (.gpx in track format) in the free version only the first 25 Track points will be saved. Auto save to _LastCreatedTrack.gpx in the open file list.\r\nNow it’s possible to measure distance on map by clicking on the map two or more times. In the free version only measure thru a straight line and in pro also via roads.\r\nSupport for Feedback app (require Windows 10 version 10.0.14271 or later)\r\nSupporting Windows INK, you can write with pen, mouse and touch on the map\r\nNow translated to more languages, PoiViwer10 will automatic select your language from French, German, Swedish, Spanish or Portuguese.
